### 212. ❌ Robust Wildfire Forecasting under Partial Observability: From Reconstruction to Prediction

**作者**: Chen Yang, Mehdi Zafari, Ziheng Duan, A. Lee Swindlehurst
**期刊/来源**: arxiv
**发布日期**: 2026-03-10

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文针对卫星野火观测数据不完整的问题，提出了一个两阶段概率框架，通过重建被遮挡的火灾图像并预测其时空动态，显著提高了部分可观测条件下的野火预测准确性。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 卫星获取的火情观测数据是学习型野火蔓延预测的主要输入，但由于云层覆盖、烟雾遮蔽及传感器伪影等因素，这些数据本质上是不完整的。这种部分可观测性在训练预测模型所用的洁净数据与部署时遇到的降质输入之间引入了领域差异，常导致预测结果不可靠。为应对这一挑战，我们采用一个两阶段概率框架来形式化部分可观测条件下的野火预测，该框架将观测恢复与时空预测解耦。第一阶段通过条件修复从受损观测中重建合理的火势分布图；第二阶段则使用时序预测网络基于恢复后的序列模拟野火动态。我们为重建模块考虑了四种网络架构——基于残差的U-Net（MaskUNet）、条件变分自编码器（Conditional VAE, MaskCVAE）、交叉注意力视觉Transformer（MaskViT）以及离散扩散模型（MaskD3PM），涵盖了基于CNN、隐变量、注意力机制和扩散模型的方法。我们在WildfireSpreadTS（WSTS）数据集上评估了该两阶段方法在不同设置下的性能，包括逐像素与分块掩蔽、八种损坏程度（10%-80%）、四种火情场景以及留一年交叉验证。结果表明，所有基于学习的恢复模型均显著优于非学习基线，其中MaskCVAE与MaskUNet取得了最佳整体性能。重要的是，在预测前加入重建阶段能显著缓解领域差异，即使在严重信息损失的情况下，也能将次日预测精度恢复至接近洁净输入的水平。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Satellite-derived fire observations are the primary input for learning-based wildfire spread prediction, yet they are inherently incomplete due to cloud cover, smoke obscuration, and sensor artifacts. This partial observability introduces a domain gap between the clean data used to train forecasting models and the degraded inputs encountered during deployment, often leading to unreliable predictions. To address this challenge, we formulate wildfire forecasting under partial observability using a two-stage probabilistic framework that decouples observation recovery from spatiotemporal prediction. Stage-I reconstructs plausible fire maps from corrupted observations via conditional inpainting, while Stage-II models wildfire dynamics on the recovered sequences using a spatiotemporal forecasting network. We consider four network architectures for the reconstruction module-a Residual U-Net (MaskUNet), a Conditional VAE (MaskCVAE), a cross-attention Vision Transformer (MaskViT), and a discrete diffusion model (MaskD3PM)-spanning CNN-based, latent-variable, attention-based, and diffusion-based approaches. We evaluate the performance of the two-stage approach on the WildfireSpreadTS (WSTS) dataset under various settings, including pixel-wise and block-wise masking, eight corruption levels (10%-80%), four fire scenarios, and leave-one-year-out cross-validation. Results show that all learning-based recovery models substantially outperform non-learning baselines, with MaskCVAE and MaskUNet achieving the strongest overall performance. Importantly, inserting the reconstruction stage before forecasting significantly mitigates the domain gap, restoring next-day prediction accuracy to near-clean-input levels even under severe information loss.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: wildfire forecasting, partial observability, satellite fire observations, conditional inpainting, spatiotemporal prediction, domain gap mitigation, reconstruction and prediction, probabilistic framework

### 213. ❌ OccTrack360: 4D Panoptic Occupancy Tracking from Surround-View Fisheye Cameras

**作者**: Yongzhi Lin, Kai Luo, Yuanfan Zheng, Hao Shi, Mengfei Duan, Yang Liu, Kailun Yang
**期刊/来源**: arxiv
**发布日期**: 2026-03-09

**评分理由**: 论文研究的是自动驾驶和机器人领域的4D全景占用跟踪，使用鱼眼相机进行环境感知，与医疗图像分析、医学影像分割、疾病诊断、预后预测、手术规划等医疗领域关键词完全无关。论文内容涉及计算机视觉、自动驾驶感知、3D场景理解，但未涉及任何医疗应用或医学影像数据。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文提出了OccTrack360基准和FoSOcc框架，用于解决自动驾驶中基于环视鱼眼相机的4D全景占用跟踪问题，并在实验中展示了方法在几何规则类别上的显著改进。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 在空间上连续且时间上一致地理解动态三维环境，是机器人技术和自动驾驶领域的基础。尽管近期在占据栅格预测（occupancy prediction）方面的进展为场景几何与语义提供了统一表征，但四维全景占据栅格跟踪（4D panoptic occupancy tracking）的发展仍受限于缺乏支持环视鱼眼传感、长时序序列以及实例级体素跟踪的基准数据集。为填补这一空白，我们提出了OccTrack360——一个基于环视鱼眼相机的四维全景占据栅格跟踪新基准。OccTrack360提供了比现有基准更长且更多样化的序列（174~2234帧），并配备了经过严谨标注的体素可见性信息，包括全向遮挡掩码和基于MEI（Mei模型）的鱼眼视场掩码。为建立一个面向鱼眼相机的强基线方法，我们进一步提出了Focus on Sphere Occ（FoSOcc）框架，该框架旨在解决鱼眼占据栅格跟踪中的两个核心挑战：扭曲的球面投影和不准确的体素空间定位。FoSOcc包含一个中心聚焦模块（Center Focusing Module, CFM），通过有监督的聚焦引导来增强实例感知的空间定位能力；以及一个球面提升模块（Spherical Lift Module, SLM），该模块在统一投影模型（Unified Projection Model）下将透视提升技术扩展至鱼眼成像。在Occ3D-Waymo和OccTrack360数据集上进行的大量实验表明，我们的方法显著提升了占据栅格跟踪的质量，尤其在几何规则类别上取得了明显增益，并为未来环视鱼眼四维占据栅格跟踪的研究建立了坚实的基线。该基准数据集及源代码将在https://github.com/YouthZest-Lin/OccTrack360 公开。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Understanding dynamic 3D environments in a spatially continuous and temporally consistent manner is fundamental for robotics and autonomous driving. While recent advances in occupancy prediction provide a unified representation of scene geometry and semantics, progress in 4D panoptic occupancy tracking remains limited by the lack of benchmarks that support surround-view fisheye sensing, long temporal sequences, and instance-level voxel tracking. To address this gap, we present OccTrack360, a new benchmark for 4D panoptic occupancy tracking from surround-view fisheye cameras. OccTrack360 provides substantially longer and more diverse sequences (174~2234 frames) than prior benchmarks, together with principled voxel visibility annotations, including an all-direction occlusion mask and an MEI-based fisheye field-of-view mask. To establish a strong fisheye-oriented baseline, we further propose Focus on Sphere Occ (FoSOcc), a framework that addresses two core challenges in fisheye occupancy tracking: distorted spherical projection and inaccurate voxel-space localization. FoSOcc includes a Center Focusing Module (CFM) to enhance instance-aware spatial localization through supervised focus guidance, and a Spherical Lift Module (SLM) that extends perspective lifting to fisheye imaging under the Unified Projection Model. Extensive experiments on Occ3D-Waymo and OccTrack360 show that our method improves occupancy tracking quality with notable gains on geometrically regular categories, and establishes a strong baseline for future research on surround-view fisheye 4D occupancy tracking. The benchmark and source code will be made publicly available at https://github.com/YouthZest-Lin/OccTrack360.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: 4D panoptic occupancy tracking, surround-view fisheye cameras, autonomous driving, voxel tracking, spherical projection, instance-aware localization, benchmark dataset, robotics perception

### 214. ❌ Spherical-GOF: Geometry-Aware Panoramic Gaussian Opacity Fields for 3D Scene Reconstruction

**作者**: Zhe Yang, Guoqiang Zhao, Sheng Wu, Kai Luo, Kailun Yang
**期刊/来源**: arxiv
**发布日期**: 2026-03-09
**arXiv链接**: [http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08503v1](http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08503v1)

**评分**: 0.0 / 29.0 ❌

<details>
<summary>评分详情</summary>

| 关键词 | 权重 | 相关度 | 得分 |
|------|------|------|------|
| medical image analysis | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| medical image segmentation | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| deep learning medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| AI for diagnosis | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| prognosis prediction | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| surgical planning | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| multimodal medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| foundation models medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文专注于计算机视觉和机器人领域的全景3D场景重建技术（Spherical-GOF框架），涉及高斯渲染、几何一致性、全景相机模型等。所有评分关键词均针对医学影像分析、疾病诊断、手术规划等医疗AI应用，而本文完全不涉及医学领域、医疗数据或临床应用，因此所有关键词相关度均为0分。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    本文提出了Spherical-GOF框架，解决了全景相机模型下3D高斯渲染的几何失真问题，在标准数据集上显著提升了深度重建的几何一致性。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 全向图像因其宽广的视野在机器人与视觉领域中的应用日益增多。然而，将三维高斯泼溅（3DGS）扩展到全景相机模型仍具挑战性，因为现有方法均针对透视投影设计，简单的适配常会引入畸变和几何不一致性。我们提出了Spherical-GOF，一个基于高斯不透明度场（GOF）的全向高斯渲染框架。与基于投影的光栅化方法不同，Spherical-GOF直接在球面射线空间的单位球面上进行GOF射线采样，从而为全景渲染实现了一致的射线-高斯交互。为使球面射线投射高效且鲁棒，我们推导了一种用于快速射线-高斯剔除的保守球面边界规则，并引入了一种球面滤波方案，使高斯足迹能够适应畸变变化的全向像素采样。在标准全景基准数据集（OmniBlender和OmniPhotos）上的大量实验表明，本方法在光度质量上具有竞争力，并显著提升了几何一致性。与最强基线相比，Spherical-GOF将深度重投影误差降低了57%，并将循环内点比率提高了21%。定性结果显示更清晰的深度图和更连贯的法线图，且对全局全景旋转具有强鲁棒性。我们进一步在OmniRob数据集上验证了泛化能力，该数据集是本工作中引入的真实世界机器人全向数据集，包含无人机和四足机器人平台。源代码与OmniRob数据集将在https://github.com/1170632760/Spherical-GOF发布。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Omnidirectional images are increasingly used in robotics and vision due to their wide field of view. However, extending 3D Gaussian Splatting (3DGS) to panoramic camera models remains challenging, as existing formulations are designed for perspective projections and naive adaptations often introduce distortion and geometric inconsistencies. We present Spherical-GOF, an omnidirectional Gaussian rendering framework built upon Gaussian Opacity Fields (GOF). Unlike projection-based rasterization, Spherical-GOF performs GOF ray sampling directly on the unit sphere in spherical ray space, enabling consistent ray-Gaussian interactions for panoramic rendering. To make the spherical ray casting efficient and robust, we derive a conservative spherical bounding rule for fast ray-Gaussian culling and introduce a spherical filtering scheme that adapts Gaussian footprints to distortion-varying panoramic pixel sampling. Extensive experiments on standard panoramic benchmarks (OmniBlender and OmniPhotos) demonstrate competitive photometric quality and substantially improved geometric consistency. Compared with the strongest baseline, Spherical-GOF reduces depth reprojection error by 57% and improves cycle inlier ratio by 21%. Qualitative results show cleaner depth and more coherent normal maps, with strong robustness to global panorama rotations. We further validate generalization on OmniRob, a real-world robotic omnidirectional dataset introduced in this work, featuring UAV and quadruped platforms. The source code and the OmniRob dataset will be released at https://github.com/1170632760/Spherical-GOF.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: 3D scene reconstruction, panoramic rendering, Gaussian Opacity Fields, spherical ray sampling, geometric consistency, omnidirectional images, depth reprojection error, robotics vision

---

### 215. ❌ Bootstrapping Audiovisual Speech Recognition in Zero-AV-Resource Scenarios with Synthetic Visual Data

**作者**: Pol Buitrago, Pol Gàlvez, Oriol Pareras, Javier Hernando
**期刊/来源**: arxiv
**发布日期**: 2026-03-09

**评分**: 0.0 / 29.0 ❌

|------|------|------|------|

| multimodal medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文研究的是视听语音识别（AVSR），属于计算机视觉和语音处理的交叉领域，具体涉及通过合成视觉数据（唇部同步）来提升低资源语言的语音识别性能。研究背景明确指向医学影像分析和临床决策支持，包括CT、MRI、超声等医学影像的分割、诊断、预后预测、手术规划等。论文内容完全不涉及医学影像、疾病诊断、手术规划或任何医疗应用，所有关键词均与论文主题无关。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文提出了一种零视听资源场景下的视听语音识别框架，通过合成唇部同步视频数据，在缺乏标注视频语料的加泰罗尼亚语上实现了接近最先进的性能，并证明了合成视频在噪声环境下保持多模态优势。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 视听语音识别（AVSR）通过结合声学与视觉线索来提升嘈杂环境下的转录鲁棒性，但由于缺乏用于训练的标注视频语料库，该技术对大多数资源匮乏的语言仍难以实现。我们提出了一种零视听资源AVSR框架，该框架依赖于通过真实音频对口型静态面部图像生成的合成视觉流。我们首先在西班牙语基准测试中评估合成视觉增强的效果，随后将其应用于缺乏标注视听语料库的加泰罗尼亚语。我们合成了超过700小时的说话人头部视频，并对预训练的AV-HuBERT模型进行微调。在人工标注的加泰罗尼亚语基准测试中，我们的模型以更少的参数量和训练数据实现了接近最先进的性能，优于在相同条件下训练的纯音频基线模型，并在噪声环境中保持了多模态优势。因此，可扩展的合成视频为零视听资源AVSR提供了真实录音的可行替代方案。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Audiovisual speech recognition (AVSR) combines acoustic and visual cues to improve transcription robustness under challenging conditions but remains out of reach for most under-resourced languages due to the lack of labeled video corpora for training. We propose a zero-AV-resource AVSR framework that relies on synthetic visual streams generated by lip-syncing static facial images with real audio.
>   We first evaluate synthetic visual augmentation on Spanish benchmarks, then apply it to Catalan, a language with no annotated audiovisual corpora. We synthesize over 700 hours of talking-head video and fine-tune a pre-trained AV-HuBERT model. On a manually annotated Catalan benchmark, our model achieves near state-of-the-art performance with much fewer parameters and training data, outperforms an identically trained audio-only baseline, and preserves multimodal advantages in noise. Scalable synthetic video thus offers a viable substitute for real recordings in zero-AV-resource AVSR.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: audiovisual speech recognition, zero-resource scenarios, synthetic visual data, lip-syncing, AV-HuBERT, multimodal robustness, Catalan language, video synthesis

### 216. ❌ 3-D Near-Field Passive Radar Imaging Using Multiple Illumination Sources

**作者**: Quanfeng Wang, Mei Song Tong, Thomas F. Eibert
**期刊/来源**: arxiv
**发布日期**: 2026-03-09
**arXiv链接**: [http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08217v1](http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08217v1)

**评分**: 0.0 / 29.0 ❌

<details>
<summary>评分详情</summary>

| 关键词 | 权重 | 相关度 | 得分 |
|------|------|------|------|
| medical image analysis | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| medical image segmentation | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| deep learning medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| AI for diagnosis | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| prognosis prediction | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| surgical planning | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| multimodal medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| foundation models medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文研究的是近场被动雷达成像技术，使用多个非合作发射源来增强复杂物体的成像质量。该论文属于雷达信号处理、电磁成像领域，与医学图像分析、深度学习、AI诊断、手术规划等医学应用完全无关。所有关键词均涉及医疗领域的具体应用，而本文专注于雷达物理成像方法，没有任何医学或临床相关内容。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文提出了一种使用多个非合作发射源进行近场被动雷达成像的方法，通过相干叠加不同照射配置的单频图像来减少伪影并提高复杂物体（如二面角结构）的成像质量，仿真和测量结果验证了该方法的有效性。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 近场（NF）无源雷达成像依赖于非合作发射机（Tx）对成像场景的照射。研究表明，结合不同发射天线位置获得的成像结果能够提升无源雷达成像的性能。一方面，多部发射天线提供了多样化的照射视角，降低了感兴趣目标（TOIs）上出现未照射区域的可能性。另一方面，对不同照射条件下获得的成像结果进行相干叠加，有助于抑制潜在的伪影。这种方法尤其适用于对具有凹面结构（例如二面角结构）的复杂物体进行成像，因为此类目标的多重反射伪影高度依赖于照射构型。针对每一种照射构型，采用单频逆源求解器来重建感兴趣目标的等效源，随后通过相应的相位与幅度校正方法，将所得的单频图像进行相干叠加。最终，将获得的多频图像进行相干融合，以提升成像质量。本文通过仿真与实测结果验证了该方法的有效性。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Near-field (NF) passive radar imaging depends on the illumination of the imaging scene by a non-cooperative transmitter (Tx). It is demonstrated that combining imaging results obtained with Tx antennas at different positions can enhance the performance of passive radar imaging. On the one hand, multiple Tx antennas provide diverse illumination perspectives, reducing the likelihood of unilluminated regions on the targets of interest (TOIs). On the other hand, the coherent summation of imaging results obtained for different illuminations helps to suppress potential artifacts. This approach is in particular advantageous for imaging complex objects with concave structures such as dihedral arrangements, where the ghosts due to multiple reflections are highly configuration-dependent. For each illuminating configuration, a single-frequency inverse source solver is utilized to reconstruct the equivalent sources of the TOIs and the resulting single-frequency images are then superimposed coherently with corresponding phase and magnitude correction methods. The obtained multi-frequency images are finally coherently combined to enhance the imaging quality. Both simulation and measurement results are presented to validate the effectiveness of the approach.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: near-field passive radar imaging, multiple illumination sources, non-cooperative transmitter, coherent summation, inverse source solver, complex objects imaging, artifact suppression, multi-frequency imaging

---

### 217. ❌ HiDE: Hierarchical Dictionary-Based Entropy Modeling for Learned Image Compression

**作者**: Haoxuan Xiong, Yuanyuan Xu, Kun Zhu, Yiming Wang, Baoliu Ye
**期刊/来源**: arxiv
**发布日期**: 2026-03-06
**arXiv链接**: [http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06766v1](http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06766v1)

**评分**: 0.0 / 29.0 ❌

<details>
<summary>评分详情</summary>

**评分理由**: 论文《HiDE: Hierarchical Dictionary-Based Entropy Modeling for Learned Image Compression》专注于通用图像压缩技术，提出了一种基于分层字典的熵建模框架，以提高压缩效率。研究内容涉及深度学习、熵建模、字典学习、图像压缩等计算机视觉和信号处理领域，但全文未提及任何医学图像、临床决策、疾病诊断、手术规划或医疗应用。所有评分关键词均与医学图像分析和医疗AI相关，而该论文的研究领域、方法、实验数据集（Kodak, CLIC, Tecnick）和应用场景均与医学无关，因此所有关键词的相关度均为0分。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文针对学习型图像压缩中外部先验利用不足的问题，提出了分层字典熵建模框架HiDE，在多个数据集上实现了显著的码率节省。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 学习型图像压缩（LIC）已取得显著的编码效率，其中熵建模通过信息先验在最小化码率方面发挥着关键作用。现有方法主要利用输入图像的内部上下文，而嵌入大规模训练数据中的丰富外部先验在很大程度上仍未得到充分利用。基于字典的熵模型的最新进展表明，引入外部先验可大幅提升压缩性能。然而，当前方法将异构外部先验组织在单层字典中，导致利用不均衡且表示能力有限。此外，有效的熵建模不仅需要表达力强的先验，还需要能够解读这些先验的参数估计网络。为应对这些挑战，我们提出HiDE——一种用于学习型图像压缩的基于分层字典的熵建模框架。HiDE通过级联检索将外部先验分解为全局结构字典与局部细节字典，实现了外部信息的结构化高效利用。此外，我们引入了具有并行多感受野设计的上下文感知参数估计器，以自适应地利用异构上下文进行精确的条件概率估计。实验结果表明，在Kodak、CLIC和Tecnick数据集上，HiDE相较于VTM-12.1分别实现了18.5%、21.99%和24.01%的BD-rate节省。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Learned image compression (LIC) has achieved remarkable coding efficiency, where entropy modeling plays a pivotal role in minimizing bitrate through informative priors. Existing methods predominantly exploit internal contexts within the input image, yet the rich external priors embedded in large-scale training data remain largely underutilized. Recent advances in dictionary-based entropy models have demonstrated that incorporating external priors can substantially enhance compression performance. However, current approaches organize heterogeneous external priors within a single-level dictionary, resulting in imbalanced utilization and limited representational capacity. Moreover, effective entropy modeling requires not only expressive priors but also a parameter estimation network capable of interpreting them. To address these challenges, we propose HiDE, a Hierarchical Dictionary-based Entropy modeling framework for learned image compression. HiDE decomposes external priors into global structural and local detail dictionaries with cascaded retrieval, enabling structured and efficient utilization of external information. Moreover, a context-aware parameter estimator with parallel multi-receptive-field design is introduced to adaptively exploit heterogeneous contexts for accurate conditional probability estimation. Experimental results show that HiDE achieves 18.5%, 21.99%, and 24.01% BD-rate savings over VTM-12.1 on the Kodak, CLIC, and Tecnick datasets, respectively.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: learned image compression, entropy modeling, hierarchical dictionary, external priors, bitrate reduction, deep learning, image coding, conditional probability estimation

### 218. ❌ Can we Trust Unreliable Voxels? Exploring 3D Semantic Occupancy Prediction under Label Noise

**作者**: Wenxin Li, Kunyu Peng, Di Wen, Junwei Zheng, Jiale Wei, Mengfei Duan, Yuheng Zhang, Rui Fan, Kailun Yang
**期刊/来源**: arxiv
**发布日期**: 2026-03-06
**arXiv链接**: [http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06279v1](http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06279v1)

**评分**: 0.0 / 29.0 ❌

<details>
<summary>评分详情</summary>

|------|------|------|------|

| prognosis prediction | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

| foundation models medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文研究3D语义占用预测在标签噪声下的鲁棒性问题，属于机器人感知和自动驾驶领域，核心内容包括3D语义占用预测、标签噪声学习、基准测试（OccNL）和鲁棒框架（DPR-Occ）。所有评分关键词均针对医学影像分析和临床决策支持，而论文未涉及任何医学影像（如CT、MRI、超声）、疾病诊断、预后预测或手术规划，因此与所有关键词完全无关，评分均为0。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文研究了3D语义占用预测在标签噪声下的可靠性问题，提出了首个基准OccNL和鲁棒框架DPR-Occ，在极端噪声下显著提升了性能。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 三维语义占据预测是机器人感知的基石，然而现实世界中的体素标注本质上受到结构伪影和动态拖尾效应的干扰。这引发了一个关键但尚未被充分探索的问题：自主系统能否安全地依赖这种不可靠的占据监督？为系统性地研究此问题，我们建立了OccNL——首个专门针对占据不对称和动态拖尾噪声下的三维占据预测的基准。我们的分析揭示了一个根本性的领域差距：最先进的二维标签噪声学习策略在稀疏的三维体素空间中会灾难性地失效，暴露出现有范式的关键脆弱性。为应对这一挑战，我们提出了DPR-Occ，一个基于原理的标签噪声鲁棒性框架，它通过双源部分标签推理构建可靠的监督。通过将时序模型记忆与表征层面的结构亲和性相协同，DPR-Occ动态地扩展和修剪候选标签集，以保留真实语义并抑制噪声传播。在SemanticKITTI数据集上的大量实验表明，DPR-Occ能在极端噪声下防止几何和语义崩溃。值得注意的是，即使在90%的标签噪声下，我们的方法相较于为三维占据预测任务调整的现有标签噪声学习基线，仍实现了显著的性能提升（最高达2.57% mIoU和13.91% IoU）。通过连接标签噪声学习与三维感知，OccNL和DPR-Occ为动态环境中安全关键的机器人感知提供了可靠的基础。基准测试和源代码将在https://github.com/mylwx/OccNL公开提供。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> 3D semantic occupancy prediction is a cornerstone of robotic perception, yet real-world voxel annotations are inherently corrupted by structural artifacts and dynamic trailing effects. This raises a critical but underexplored question: can autonomous systems safely rely on such unreliable occupancy supervision? To systematically investigate this issue, we establish OccNL, the first benchmark dedicated to 3D occupancy under occupancy-asymmetric and dynamic trailing noise. Our analysis reveals a fundamental domain gap: state-of-the-art 2D label noise learning strategies collapse catastrophically in sparse 3D voxel spaces, exposing a critical vulnerability in existing paradigms. To address this challenge, we propose DPR-Occ, a principled label noise-robust framework that constructs reliable supervision through dual-source partial label reasoning. By synergizing temporal model memory with representation-level structural affinity, DPR-Occ dynamically expands and prunes candidate label sets to preserve true semantics while suppressing noise propagation. Extensive experiments on SemanticKITTI demonstrate that DPR-Occ prevents geometric and semantic collapse under extreme corruption. Notably, even at 90% label noise, our method achieves significant performance gains (up to 2.57% mIoU and 13.91% IoU) over existing label noise learning baselines adapted to the 3D occupancy prediction task. By bridging label noise learning and 3D perception, OccNL and DPR-Occ provide a reliable foundation for safety-critical robotic perception in dynamic environments. The benchmark and source code will be made publicly available at https://github.com/mylwx/OccNL.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: 3D semantic occupancy prediction, label noise, robust perception, benchmark, autonomous systems, deep learning, robotic perception, voxel annotations

### 219. ❌ NOVA: Next-step Open-Vocabulary Autoregression for 3D Multi-Object Tracking in Autonomous Driving

**作者**: Kai Luo, Xu Wang, Rui Fan, Kailun Yang
**期刊/来源**: arxiv
**发布日期**: 2026-03-06
**arXiv链接**: [http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06254v1](http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06254v1)

**评分**: 0.0 / 29.0 ❌

<details>
<summary>评分详情</summary>

| 关键词 | 权重 | 相关度 | 得分 |
|------|------|------|------|
| medical image analysis | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| medical image segmentation | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| deep learning medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| AI for diagnosis | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| prognosis prediction | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| surgical planning | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| multimodal medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| foundation models medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文研究的是自动驾驶领域的3D多目标跟踪（3D MOT），使用大语言模型（LLMs）进行开放词汇自回归轨迹生成。所有评分关键词均与医学图像分析、临床决策支持、疾病诊断/预后、手术规划等医疗领域相关，而本文完全不涉及任何医疗或医学影像内容，专注于自动驾驶的计算机视觉和自然语言处理交叉应用。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文提出了一种名为NOVA的开放词汇自回归范式，用于解决自动驾驶中3D多目标跟踪的语义泛化问题，通过在nuScenes等数据集上实现显著的性能提升（如新类别AMOTA提高20.21%）。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 在开放世界感知中，对未知目标的泛化能力至关重要，然而现有的三维多目标跟踪（3D MOT）流程仍受限于闭集假设和“语义盲”启发式方法。为解决这一问题，我们提出了“下一步开放词汇自回归”（NOVA），这是一种创新范式，将三维跟踪从传统的、基于距离的碎片化匹配转向生成式时空语义建模。NOVA将三维轨迹重新定义为结构化的时空语义序列，从而能够同时编码物理运动连续性和深层语言先验。通过利用大语言模型（LLMs）的自回归能力，我们将跟踪任务转化为一种原则性的“下一步序列补全”过程。该机制使模型能够显式利用语言空间的层次结构，以解决细粒度语义歧义，并通过高层常识推理在复杂长程序列中保持身份一致性。在nuScenes、V2X-Seq-SPD和KITTI数据集上进行的大量实验验证了NOVA的卓越性能。值得注意的是，在nuScenes数据集上，NOVA在“新类别”（Novel categories）上实现了22.41%的AMOTA指标，相比基线方法获得了20.21%的绝对性能提升。这些成果是通过一个紧凑的0.5B参数自回归模型实现的。代码将在https://github.com/xifen523/NOVA 公开。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Generalizing across unknown targets is critical for open-world perception, yet existing 3D Multi-Object Tracking (3D MOT) pipelines remain limited by closed-set assumptions and ``semantic-blind'' heuristics. To address this, we propose Next-step Open-Vocabulary Autoregression (NOVA), an innovative paradigm that shifts 3D tracking from traditional fragmented distance-based matching toward generative spatio-temporal semantic modeling. NOVA reformulates 3D trajectories as structured spatio-temporal semantic sequences, enabling the simultaneous encoding of physical motion continuity and deep linguistic priors. By leveraging the autoregressive capabilities of Large Language Models (LLMs), we transform the tracking task into a principled process of next-step sequence completion. This mechanism allows the model to explicitly utilize the hierarchical structure of language space to resolve fine-grained semantic ambiguities and maintain identity consistency across complex long-range sequences through high-level commonsense reasoning. Extensive experiments on nuScenes, V2X-Seq-SPD, and KITTI demonstrate the superior performance of NOVA. Notably, on the nuScenes dataset, NOVA achieves an AMOTA of 22.41% for Novel categories, yielding a significant 20.21% absolute improvement over the baseline. These gains are realized through a compact 0.5B autoregressive model. Code will be available at https://github.com/xifen523/NOVA.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: 3D Multi-Object Tracking, open-vocabulary, autoregression, Large Language Models, spatio-temporal semantic modeling, autonomous driving, trajectory generation, semantic ambiguity resolution

### 220. ❌ Enhancing Neural Video Compression of Static Scenes with Positive-Incentive Noise

**作者**: Cheng Yuan, Zhenyu Jia, Jiawei Shao, Xuelong Li
**期刊/来源**: arxiv
**发布日期**: 2026-03-06
**arXiv链接**: [http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06095v1](http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06095v1)

**评分**: 0.0 / 29.0 ❌

<details>
<summary>评分详情</summary>

| 关键词 | 权重 | 相关度 | 得分 |
|------|------|------|------|
| medical image analysis | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| medical image segmentation | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| deep learning medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| AI for diagnosis | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| prognosis prediction | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| surgical planning | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| multimodal medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| foundation models medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文研究的是静态场景视频的神经视频压缩技术，通过引入正激励噪声来提升压缩效率，主要应用于监控视频和视频通话等通用视频领域。论文内容完全不涉及医学图像分析、医学影像分割、深度学习医学成像、AI诊断、预后预测、手术规划、多模态医学成像或医学成像基础模型等医学领域。所有关键词与论文主题无任何关联。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文提出了一种通过引入正激励噪声来提升静态场景视频神经视频压缩效率的方法，在保持像素级保真度的同时实现了73%的比特率节省。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 静态场景视频（如监控录像与视频通话流）在存储消耗与网络流量中占据主导地位。然而，传统标准化编解码器与神经视频压缩（Neural Video Compression, NVC）方法分别因时间冗余利用不足以及训练与测试数据间存在显著分布差异，难以高效编码此类视频。尽管近期生成式压缩方法提升了感知质量，但其引入的幻觉细节在真实性要求严格的应用中不可接受。为克服这些局限，我们提出将正向激励噪声引入静态场景视频的NVC框架中，其中短期时序变化被重新解读为正向激励噪声以促进模型微调。通过将瞬时变化与持久背景解耦，结构化先验信息被内化于压缩模型中。在推理阶段，不变分量仅需极少的信号传输，从而在保持像素级保真度的同时降低数据传输需求。初步实验表明，相较于通用NVC模型，本方法可实现73%的Bjøntegaard delta（BD）码率节省。该方法提供了以计算换带宽的有效解决方案，能够在恶劣网络条件下实现鲁棒视频传输，并支持监控影像的经济型长期存储。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Static scene videos, such as surveillance feeds and videotelephony streams, constitute a dominant share of storage consumption and network traffic. However, both traditional standardized codecs and neural video compression (NVC) methods struggle to encode these videos efficiently due to inadequate usage of temporal redundancy and severe distribution gaps between training and test data, respectively. While recent generative compression methods improve perceptual quality, they introduce hallucinated details that are unacceptable in authenticity-critical applications. To overcome these limitations, we propose to incorporate positive-incentive noise into NVC for static scene videos, where short-term temporal changes are reinterpreted as positive-incentive noise to facilitate model finetuning. By disentangling transient variations from the persistent background, structured prior information is internalized in the compression model. During inference, the invariant component requires minimal signaling, thus reducing data transmission while maintaining pixel-level fidelity. Preliminary experiments demonstrate a 73% Bjøntegaard delta (BD) rate saving compared to general NVC models. Our method provides an effective solution to trade computation for bandwidth, enabling robust video transmission under adverse network conditions and economic long-term retention of surveillance footage.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: neural video compression, static scene videos, positive-incentive noise, temporal redundancy, video compression efficiency, Bjøntegaard delta rate saving, surveillance footage compression, computational bandwidth trade-off

**作者**: Zunaira Shafqat, Atif Aftab Ahmed Jilani, Qurrat Ul Ain
**期刊/来源**: arxiv

**评分理由**: 论文研究的是手术器械的自动化光学检测（AOI），使用深度学习模型（YOLOv8, ResNet-152, EfficientNet-b4）检测制造缺陷（如裂纹、锈蚀）。虽然涉及深度学习和医疗领域（手术器械），但核心是工业质量检测，而非医学图像分析、疾病诊断、预后预测、手术规划或多模态医学成像。所有关键词均与医学影像分析、临床决策支持相关，而本文焦点是器械制造缺陷检测，因此所有关键词相关度为0。

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该研究开发了一个基于深度学习的自动化光学检测系统，用于识别巴基斯坦制造的手术器械的缺陷（如裂纹和锈蚀），以提高制造质量并确保手术安全。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 在现代医疗的动态格局中，维持手术器械的最高标准对临床成功至关重要。本报告探讨了手术器械的多样领域及其相关制造缺陷，强调了其在确保手术安全性中的关键作用。即便是微小缺陷也可能导致致命后果，因此制造精度至关重要。报告重点讨论了裂纹、锈蚀及结构异常等关键缺陷的识别与修正。此类严格审查不仅能为制造商避免重大经济损失，更重要的是能保障患者生命。通过与Sialkot手术器械产业集群中公认的行业先驱——Daddy D Pro和Dr. Frigz International的合作，我们获得了关于巴基斯坦产器械缺陷分析的宝贵见解。此次合作体现了对推进自动化缺陷检测方法的承诺，特别是通过整合包括YOLOv8、ResNet-152和EfficientNet-b4在内的深度学习架构，从而提升制造过程中的质量标准。本报告旨在识别巴基斯坦制造的各类手术器械，并利用新开发的4,414张高分辨率图像数据集分析其相关缺陷。通过聚焦基于自动光学检测（Automated Optical Inspection, AOI）工具的质量保证，本文档为制造商、医疗专业人员和监管机构提供了重要参考。所获见解有助于提升器械标准，借助行业专业知识与前沿技术，共同构建更可靠的医疗环境。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> In the dynamic landscape of modern healthcare, maintaining the highest standards in surgical instruments is critical for clinical success. This report explores the diverse realm of surgical instruments and their associated manufacturing defects, emphasizing their pivotal role in ensuring the safety of surgical procedures. With potentially fatal consequences arising from even minor defects, precision in manufacturing is paramount.The report addresses the identification and rectification of critical defects such as cracks, rust, and structural irregularities. Such scrutiny prevents substantial financial losses for manufacturers and, more crucially, safeguards patient lives. The collaboration with industry leaders Daddy D Pro and Dr. Frigz International, renowned trailblazers in the Sialkot surgical cluster, provides invaluable insights into the analysis of defects in Pakistani-made instruments. This partnership signifies a commitment to advancing automated defect detection methodologies, specifically through the integration of deep learning architectures including YOLOv8, ResNet-152, and EfficientNet-b4, thereby elevating quality standards in the manufacturing process. The scope of this report is to identify various surgical instruments manufactured in Pakistan and analyze their associated defects using a newly developed dataset of 4,414 high-resolution images. By focusing on quality assurance through Automated Optical Inspection (AOI) tools, this document serves as a resource for manufacturers, healthcare professionals, and regulatory bodies. The insights gained contribute to the enhancement of instrument standards, ensuring a more reliable healthcare environment through industry expertise and cutting-edge technology.

</details>

**关键词**: Automated Optical Inspection, surgical instruments, defect detection, deep learning, YOLOv8, quality assurance, manufacturing defects, industrial collaboration

### 222. ❌ Architectural Unification for Polarimetric Imaging Across Multiple Degradations

**作者**: Chu Zhou, Yufei Han, Junda Liao, Linrui Dai, Wangze Xu, Art Subpa-Asa, Heng Guo, Boxin Shi, Imari Sato
**期刊/来源**: arxiv
**发布日期**: 2026-03-06
**arXiv链接**: [http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05834v1](http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05834v1)

**评分**: 0.0 / 29.0 ❌

<details>
<summary>评分详情</summary>

| 关键词 | 权重 | 相关度 | 得分 |
|------|------|------|------|
| medical image analysis | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| medical image segmentation | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| deep learning medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| AI for diagnosis | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| prognosis prediction | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| surgical planning | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| multimodal medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| foundation models medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文研究偏振成像（polarimetric imaging）的参数恢复问题，专注于处理低光噪声、运动模糊和马赛克伪影等退化问题，提出统一的架构框架进行图像-Stokes联合处理。所有评分关键词均涉及医学影像分析、深度学习医学成像、AI诊断、预后预测、手术规划、多模态医学成像和医学影像基础模型等医疗健康领域的具体应用。论文内容完全属于计算机视觉和计算成像领域，与医学影像或临床决策支持无任何关联。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文提出了一种统一的架构框架，用于从退化的偏振测量中恢复物理一致的偏振参数，在低光去噪、运动去模糊和去马赛克任务上实现了最先进的性能。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 偏振成像旨在从捕获的偏振测量数据中恢复偏振参数，包括总强度（Total Intensity, TI）、偏振度（Degree of Polarization, DoP）和偏振角（Angle of Polarization, AoP）。在实际场景中，这些测量数据常受到多种退化效应的影响，如低光噪声、运动模糊和马赛克伪影。由于DoP和AoP与测量强度之间存在非线性依赖关系，从退化的观测数据中准确恢复物理一致的偏振参数仍极具挑战。现有方法通常采用针对单一退化类型设计的专用网络架构，限制了其在不同复原场景中的适应性。此外，许多方法依赖于多阶段处理流程，易产生误差累积，或仅在单一域（图像域或斯托克斯域）中操作，未能充分利用两者之间的内在物理关联。本研究提出一种用于偏振成像的统一架构框架，该框架在多种退化场景中共享结构设计。我们无需为每项任务重新设计网络结构，而是保持一致的架构，仅针对不同退化类型进行分别训练。该模型执行单阶段的图像-斯托克斯联合处理，避免了误差累积，并显式保持了物理一致性。大量实验表明，这种统一架构在针对特定退化类型训练后，在低光去噪、运动去模糊和解马赛克任务中均能持续取得最先进的性能，为退化偏振成像提供了一个通用且基于物理原理的解决方案。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Polarimetric imaging aims to recover polarimetric parameters, including Total Intensity (TI), Degree of Polarization (DoP), and Angle of Polarization (AoP), from captured polarized measurements. In real-world scenarios, these measurements are frequently affected by diverse degradations such as low-light noise, motion blur, and mosaicing artifacts. Due to the nonlinear dependency of DoP and AoP on the measured intensities, accurately retrieving physically consistent polarimetric parameters from degraded observations remains highly challenging. Existing approaches typically adopt task-specific network architectures tailored to individual degradation types, limiting their adaptability across different restoration scenarios. Moreover, many methods rely on multi-stage processing pipelines that suffer from error accumulation, or operate solely in a single domain (either image or Stokes domain), failing to fully exploit the intrinsic physical relationships between them. In this work, we propose a unified architectural framework for polarimetric imaging that is structurally shared across multiple degradation scenarios. Rather than redesigning network structures for each task, our framework maintains a consistent architectural design while being trained separately for different degradations. The model performs single-stage joint image-Stokes processing, avoiding error accumulation and explicitly preserving physical consistency. Extensive experiments show that this unified architectural design, when trained for specific degradation types, consistently achieves state-of-the-art performance across low-light denoising, motion deblurring, and demosaicing tasks, establishing a versatile and physically grounded solution for degraded polarimetric imaging.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: polarimetric imaging, unified architectural framework, degradation restoration, image-Stokes joint processing, physical consistency, low-light denoising, motion deblurring, demosaicing

### 223. ❌ Uni-LVC: A Unified Method for Intra- and Inter-Mode Learned Video Compression

**作者**: Yichi Zhang, Ruoyu Yang, Fengqing Zhu
**期刊/来源**: arxiv
**发布日期**: 2026-03-05
**arXiv链接**: [http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05756v1](http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05756v1)

**评分**: 0.0 / 29.0 ❌

<details>
<summary>评分详情</summary>

| 关键词 | 权重 | 相关度 | 得分 |
|------|------|------|------|
| medical image analysis | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| medical image segmentation | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| deep learning medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| AI for diagnosis | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| prognosis prediction | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| surgical planning | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| multimodal medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| foundation models medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文《Uni-LVC: A Unified Method for Intra- and Inter-Mode Learned Video Compression》专注于视频压缩技术，特别是基于学习的视频编解码器（LVC）。研究内容涉及统一帧内和帧间编码模式、跨注意力机制、可靠性感知分类器、多阶段训练策略等，旨在提高压缩效率和鲁棒性。所有评分关键词均与医学影像分析、疾病诊断、手术规划等医疗AI应用相关，而该论文完全不涉及医疗领域、医学影像或临床决策支持。因此，所有关键词的相关度均为0分。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文提出了一种统一的基于学习的视频压缩方法Uni-LVC，通过跨注意力适应模块和可靠性感知分类器，在单一模型中支持帧内和帧间编码，实现了优异的率失真性能和计算效率。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 近年来，学习型视频压缩（LVC）领域的最新进展带来了显著的性能提升，其中如DCVC-RT等编解码器在压缩效率上已超越H.266/VVC的低延迟模式。然而，现有LVC方法仍存在关键局限：它们通常需要为帧内和帧间编码模式分别训练独立模型，且在时间参考帧不可靠时性能会下降。为解决这些问题，我们提出了Uni-LVC，这是一种统一的LVC方法，能够在单一模型中同时支持低延迟和随机访问模式下的帧内与帧间编码。基于一个强大的帧内编解码器，Uni-LVC将帧间编码构建为以参考帧中提取的时间信息为条件的帧内编码。我们设计了一个高效的交叉注意力自适应模块，用于整合时间线索，从而无缝支持单向（低延迟）和双向（随机访问）预测模式。此外，我们提出了一种可靠性感知分类器，用于有选择地缩放时间线索，使得当参考帧不可靠时，Uni-LVC的行为更接近于帧内编码。我们还进一步提出了一种多阶段训练策略，以促进跨不同编码模式的自适应学习。大量实验表明，Uni-LVC在帧内和帧间配置下均实现了优异的率失真性能，同时保持了可比较的计算效率。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Recent advances in learned video compression (LVC) have led to significant performance gains, with codecs such as DCVC-RT surpassing the H.266/VVC low-delay mode in compression efficiency. However, existing LVCs still exhibit key limitations: they often require separate models for intra and inter coding modes, and their performance degrades when temporal references are unreliable. To address this, we introduce Uni-LVC, a unified LVC method that supports both intra and inter coding with low-delay and random-access in a single model. Building on a strong intra-codec, Uni-LVC formulates inter-coding as intra-coding conditioned on temporal information extracted from reference frames. We design an efficient cross-attention adaptation module that integrates temporal cues, enabling seamless support for both unidirectional (low-delay) and bidirectional (random-access) prediction modes. A reliability-aware classifier is proposed to selectively scale the temporal cues, making Uni-LVC behave closer to intra coding when references are unreliable. We further propose a multistage training strategy to facilitate adaptive learning across various coding modes. Extensive experiments demonstrate that Uni-LVC achieves superior rate-distortion performance in intra and inter configurations while maintaining comparable computational efficiency.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: learned video compression, intra-coding, inter-coding, cross-attention adaptation, reliability-aware classifier, rate-distortion performance, unified model, temporal reference

---

### 224. ❌ Adaptive Sampling for Storage of Progressive Images on DNA

**作者**: Xavier Pic, Nimesh Pinnamaneni, Raja Appuswamy
**期刊/来源**: arxiv
**发布日期**: 2026-03-05
**arXiv链接**: [http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05220v1](http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05220v1)

**评分**: 0.0 / 29.0 ❌

<details>
<summary>评分详情</summary>

|------|------|------|------|
| medical image analysis | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

| deep learning medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

| prognosis prediction | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| surgical planning | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| multimodal medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| foundation models medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文研究DNA数据存储技术，专注于图像编码和存储优化，与医学图像分析、AI诊断、手术规划等医疗AI领域完全无关。所有关键词均未在标题或摘要中出现，论文主题是数据存储系统而非医疗应用。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文提出了一种基于DNA分子存储渐进式图像的方法，通过自适应采样和JPEG DNA VM编码减少读取成本，实现高效、可靠的图像检索。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 传统数据存储介质的短暂寿命，与存储需求的指数级增长，使得长期归档成为数据存储行业乃至更广泛领域的根本性难题。因此，研究者们正在寻找能够以极低成本长期存储数据的创新介质解决方案。DNA分子以其高密度、长寿命和低能量需求，已成为数字数据归档的一种可行替代方案。然而，当前的DNA数据存储技术在成本和可靠性方面仍面临挑战。因此，编码速率和错误鲁棒性对于扩大DNA存储规模并使其在技术和经济上可行至关重要。此外，编码不同文件的DNA分子通常位于同一个寡核苷酸池中。若缺乏寡核苷酸层面的随机访问解决方案，从这些混合池中解码特定文件将极不实用，因为在检索目标文件前，所有寡核苷酸都需要先进行测序和解码，这极大地恶化了读取成本。
> 
> 本文介绍了一种将图像高效编码并存储到DNA分子中的解决方案，旨在降低检索分辨率降低版本图像所需的读取成本。该图像存储系统基于JPEG2000编解码器的渐进解码功能，但可适配任何传统的渐进式编解码器。每个分辨率层均使用JPEG DNA VM编解码器编码为一组寡核苷酸，该DNA编码器旨在以高可靠性检索文件。根据所需读取的分辨率，相应调整待测序和解码的寡核苷酸组及其部分。这些寡核苷酸将在测序时，借助纳米孔测序仪提供的自适应采样方法进行选择，从而成为一种无需PCR的随机访问解决方案。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> The short lifespan of traditional data storage media, coupled with an exponential increase in storage demand, has made long-term archival a fundamental problem in the data storage industry and beyond. Consequently, researchers are looking for innovative media solutions that can store data over long time periods at a very low cost. DNA molecules, with their high density, long lifespan, and low energy needs, have emerged as a viable alternative to digital data archival. However, current DNA data storage technologies are facing challenges with respect to cost and reliability. Thus, coding rate and error robustness are critical to scale DNA storage and make it technologically and economically achievable. Moreover, the molecules of DNA that encode different files are often located in the same oligo pool. Without random access solutions at the oligo level, it is very impractical to decode a specific file from these mixed pools, as all oligos need to first be sequenced and decoded before a target file can be retrieved, which greatly deteriorates the read cost.
>   This paper introduces a solution to efficiently encode and store images into DNA molecules, that aims at reducing the read cost necessary to retrieve a resolution-reduced version of an image. This image storage system is based on the Progressive Decoding Functionality of the JPEG2000 codec but can be adapted to any conventional progressive codec. Each resolution layer is encoded into a set of oligos using the JPEG DNA VM codec, a DNA-based coder that aims at retrieving a file with a high reliability. Depending on the desired resolution to be read, the set of oligos as well as the portion of the oligos to be sequenced and decoded are adjusted accordingly. These oligos will be selected at sequencing time, with the help of the adaptive sampling method provided by the Nanopore sequencers, making it a PCR-free random access solution.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: DNA data storage, progressive images, adaptive sampling, JPEG2000, JPEG DNA VM codec, random access, Nanopore sequencers, storage efficiency

---

### 225. ❌ Generic Camera Calibration using Blurry Images

**作者**: Zezhun Shi
**期刊/来源**: arxiv

**评分理由**: 论文《Generic Camera Calibration using Blurry Images》研究的是计算机视觉中的通用相机标定技术，通过几何约束和局部参数化光照模型来估计特征位置和空间变化的点扩散函数，以解决运动模糊问题。论文内容完全聚焦于计算机视觉、相机标定和图像去模糊技术，未涉及任何医学图像分析、医学影像分割、深度学习医学成像、AI诊断、预后预测、手术规划、多模态医学成像或医学影像基础模型等主题。所有关键词与论文研究领域无直接关联。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文提出了一种使用模糊图像进行通用相机标定的方法，通过几何约束和局部参数化光照模型同时估计特征位置和空间变化的点扩散函数，有效解决了运动模糊问题。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 相机标定是三维视觉的基础。通用相机模型标定相比参数化相机标定能获得更精确的结果。然而，使用印刷标定板对通用相机模型进行标定所需图像数量远多于参数化标定，这使得运动模糊对于个体用户而言实际上难以避免。作为解决该问题的首次尝试，我们利用几何约束与局部参数化光照模型，在解决传统图像去模糊任务中无需考虑的平移模糊歧义的同时，同步估计特征点位置与空间变化的点扩散函数。实验结果验证了我们方法的有效性。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Camera calibration is the foundation of 3D vision. Generic camera calibration can yield more accurate results than parametric cam era calibration. However, calibrating a generic camera model using printed calibration boards requires far more images than parametric calibration, making motion blur practically unavoidable for individual users. As a f irst attempt to address this problem, we draw on geometric constraints and a local parametric illumination model to simultaneously estimate feature locations and spatially varying point spread functions, while re solving the translational ambiguity that need not be considered in con ventional image deblurring tasks. Experimental results validate the effectiveness of our approach.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: camera calibration, generic camera model, blurry images, geometric constraints, point spread function, image deblurring, 3D vision, motion blur

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文提出了一种基于非规则像素排列的传感器设计，通过傅里叶域重建实现无混叠的高动态范围快照成像，有效提高了图像的空间分辨率和动态范围。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 单次曝光高动态范围成像技术对于在单次曝光中捕捉场景完整动态范围至关重要，这使其在视频和动态环境中具有不可替代的价值——这些场景中的运动使得多曝光技术或复杂硬件设置无法适用。本研究提出一种基于空间可变孔径的单次曝光高动态范围成像传感器，该传感器通过组合两种不同尺寸的原型像素实现。与标准高分辨率传感器相比，不同光敏区域通过物理方式将动态范围向低照度端扩展。为减轻混叠效应并克服因较大原型像素增加光敏区域而导致的空间分辨率损失，本研究建议采用非规则像素排列方式。通过在傅里叶域进行后续重建——该域中自然图像可稀疏表示——能够恢复高细节图像。本研究对采用非规则高动态范围传感器的图像采集方法进行了仿真分析，特别聚焦于空间分辨率特性。结果表明，该单次曝光高动态范围传感器架构能有效获取无混叠伪影的高动态范围图像。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Snapshot HDR imaging is essential to capture the full dynamic range of a scene in a single exposure, making it essential for video and dynamic environments where motion prevents the use of multi-exposure techniques or complex hardware set-ups. This work presents a snapshot HDR imaging sensor that is based on spatially varying apertures, implemented by combining two differently sized prototype pixels. The different light integration areas physically extend the dynamic range towards the lower end, compared to a standard high resolution sensor. A non-regular pixel arrangement is suggested, to mitigate aliasing and overcome a loss in spatial resolution that is associated with increased light integration area of the larger prototype pixel. Subsequent reconstruction in the Fourier domain, where natural images can be sparsely represented allows to recover the image with high detail. The image acquisition approach with the proposed non-regular HDR sensor is simulated and analysed with special emphasis on the spatial resolution. The results suggest the snapshot HDR sensor layout to be an effective way to acquire images with high dynamic range and free from aliasing artefacts.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: snapshot HDR imaging, non-regular pixel arrangement, anti-aliasing, spatially varying apertures, Fourier domain reconstruction, dynamic range extension, image sensor design, spatial resolution

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文开发了一种基于多摄像头系统和改进RT-DETR算法的紧急车辆蓝光检测系统，在测试中达到94.7%的准确率，旨在提升ADAS和道路安全。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 本研究提出了一种用于检测紧急车辆蓝色警示灯的先进系统，该系统基于ABLDataset开发——这是一个包含各种气候和地理条件下欧洲紧急车辆图像的精选数据集。系统采用四台鱼眼摄像头配置，每台摄像头水平视场角为180度，安装于车辆侧面。通过校准过程实现了检测结果的方位角定位。此外，研究对主流深度神经网络算法进行了比较分析，包括YOLO（v5、v8和v10）、RetinaNet、Faster R-CNN和RT-DETR。最终选择RT-DETR作为基础模型，并通过引入颜色注意力模块进行增强，在测试集上实现了94.7%的准确率和94.1%的召回率，现场测试检测距离可达70米。进一步地，系统通过几何变换估算紧急车辆相对于本车中心的接近角度。该系统设计用于集成到结合视觉与声学数据的多模态系统中，已展现出高效性能，为增强高级驾驶辅助系统（ADAS）和提升道路安全提供了具有前景的解决方案。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> This study presents an advanced system for detecting blue lights on emergency vehicles, developed using ABLDataset, a curated dataset that includes images of European emergency vehicles under various climatic and geographic conditions. The system employs a configuration of four fisheye cameras, each with a 180-degree horizontal field of view, mounted on the sides of the vehicle. A calibration process enables the azimuthal localization of the detections. Additionally, a comparative analysis of major deep neural network algorithms was conducted, including YOLO (v5, v8, and v10), RetinaNet, Faster R-CNN, and RT-DETR. RT-DETR was selected as the base model and enhanced through the incorporation of a color attention block, achieving an accuracy of 94.7 percent and a recall of 94.1 percent on the test set, with field test detections reaching up to 70 meters. Furthermore, the system estimates the approach angle of the emergency vehicle relative to the center of the car using geometric transformations. Designed for integration into a multimodal system that combines visual and acoustic data, this system has demonstrated high efficiency, offering a promising approach to enhancing Advanced Driver Assistance Systems (ADAS) and road safety.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: emergency vehicle detection, blue light detection, multi-camera system, RT-DETR, color attention block, ADAS, road safety, deep learning

### 228. ❌ When Denoising Becomes Unsigning: Theoretical and Empirical Analysis of Watermark Fragility Under Diffusion-Based Image Editing

**作者**: Fai Gu, Qiyu Tang, Te Wen, Emily Davis, Finn Carter
**期刊/来源**: arxiv
**发布日期**: 2026-03-05

**评分**: 0.0 / 29.0 ❌

|------|------|------|------|

| prognosis prediction | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| surgical planning | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| multimodal medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| foundation models medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文研究扩散模型图像编辑对数字水印的破坏机制，属于计算机视觉、信息安全、生成式AI领域，与医学图像分析、临床决策支持完全无关。论文未涉及任何医学影像、疾病诊断、手术规划或医疗AI模型的内容。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文研究发现扩散模型图像编辑会系统性地破坏鲁棒数字水印机制，导致水印信息在编辑过程中衰减至无法解码。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 鲁棒隐形水印系统旨在嵌入不可感知的有效载荷，使其在JPEG压缩、裁剪和加性噪声等常见后处理后仍可解码。与此同时，基于扩散模型的图像编辑技术已迅速成熟，成为现代内容处理流程中的默认转换层，实现了基于指令的编辑、对象插入与合成以及交互式几何操控。本文研究了这两种趋势之间一种微妙但日益重要的相互作用：基于扩散的编辑过程可能会无意中破坏那些为抵抗传统失真而专门设计的鲁棒水印机制，在极端情况下甚至可能使其近乎失效。我们提出了一个关于扩散编辑器的统一视角，该视角认为其（i）在潜在空间中注入大量高斯噪声，并（ii）通过学习的去噪动态投影回自然图像流形。在此视角下，水印有效载荷表现为低能量、高频信号，它们在前向扩散步骤中被系统性衰减，随后在反向生成过程中被视为干扰性变异。我们使用信息论工具形式化了这种退化过程，证明对于广泛的像素级水印编码器/解码器而言，随着编辑强度的增加，水印有效载荷与编辑后输出之间的互信息会衰减至接近零，导致解码错误率接近随机猜测。我们通过一个现实的假设性实验方案以及涵盖代表性水印方法和代表性扩散编辑器的数据表格对理论分析进行了补充。最后，我们讨论了伦理影响、负责任的披露规范，以及在生成式转换时代仍能保持效用的水印方案的具体设计准则。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Robust invisible watermarking systems aim to embed imperceptible payloads that remain decodable after common post-processing such as JPEG compression, cropping, and additive noise. In parallel, diffusion-based image editing has rapidly matured into a default transformation layer for modern content pipelines, enabling instruction-based editing, object insertion and composition, and interactive geometric manipulation. This paper studies a subtle but increasingly consequential interaction between these trends: diffusion-based editing procedures may unintentionally compromise, and in extreme cases practically bypass, robust watermarking mechanisms that were explicitly engineered to survive conventional distortions. We develop a unified view of diffusion editors that (i) inject substantial Gaussian noise in a latent space and (ii) project back to the natural image manifold via learned denoising dynamics. Under this view, watermark payloads behave as low-energy, high-frequency signals that are systematically attenuated by the forward diffusion step and then treated as nuisance variation by the reverse generative process. We formalize this degradation using information-theoretic tools, proving that for broad classes of pixel-level watermark encoders/decoders the mutual information between the watermark payload and the edited output decays toward zero as the editing strength increases, yielding decoding error close to random guessing. We complement the theory with a realistic hypothetical experimental protocol and tables spanning representative watermarking methods and representative diffusion editors. Finally, we discuss ethical implications, responsible disclosure norms, and concrete design guidelines for watermarking schemes that remain meaningful in the era of generative transformations.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: watermarking, diffusion models, image editing, robust watermarking, information theory, generative AI, denoising, latent space

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文提出了一个基于过滤的框架，研究在系统发育动力学中何时以及为何添加分类群能改善推断，通过分解方差减少为学习、不匹配和协方差分量，并证明了对于吸收估计量，知晓潜在吸收状态的预言机可获得分析师无法获得的事件学习保证。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 我们提出了一种基于过滤的框架，用于研究在何时以及为何增加分类单元能改善系统动力学推断。该框架通过构建观测末梢的自然排序，并对生成的过滤序列应用序贯贝叶斯分析来实现。我们将分类单元增加时期望方差减少分解为学习分量、失配分量和协方差分量，根据失配分量在路径上的行为将待估参数划分为不同学习类别，并证明对于吸收态待估参数，知晓潜在吸收状态的“先知”能够获得分析者无法获取的事件级学习保证。先知与分析者之间的差距源于不可约的假设，这些假设很可能适用于许多真实的系统动力学待估参数，从而确立了仅凭序列数据揭示潜在谱系信息的基本极限。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> We introduce a filtration-based framework for studying when and why adding taxa improves phylodynamic inference, by constructing a natural ordering of observed tips and applying sequential Bayesian analysis to the resulting filtration. We decompose the expected variance reduction on taxa addition into learning, mismatch, and covariance components, classify estimands into learning classes based on the pathwise behaviour of the mismatch, and show that for absorbing estimands an oracle who knows the latent absorption status obtains event-wise learning guarantees unavailable to the analyst. The gap between oracle and analyst is irreducible assumptions that are likely to hold for many real phylodynamic estimands, establishing a fundamental limit on what sequence data alone can reveal about the latent genealogy.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: sequential learning theory, Markov genealogy processes, phylodynamic inference, filtration-based framework, sequential Bayesian analysis, variance reduction, absorbing estimands, latent genealogy

### 230. ❌ Hydrodynamic origins of symmetric swimming strategies

**作者**: Takahiro Kanazawa, Kenta Ishimoto, Kyogo Kawaguchi
**期刊/来源**: arxiv
**发布日期**: 2026-03-09
**arXiv链接**: [http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08444v2](http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08444v2)

**评分**: 0.0 / 29.0 ❌

<details>
<summary>评分详情</summary>

| 关键词 | 权重 | 相关度 | 得分 |
|------|------|------|------|
| medical image analysis | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| medical image segmentation | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| deep learning medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| AI for diagnosis | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| prognosis prediction | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| surgical planning | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| multimodal medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| foundation models medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 该论文研究生物在粘性流体中的游泳策略和对称性原理，属于流体力学和生物物理学领域，与医学图像分析、人工智能、临床决策支持等关键词完全无关。论文未涉及任何医学成像技术、疾病诊断、手术规划或医疗AI模型的内容。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文研究了粘性流体中游泳策略的空间对称性原理，发现对称和反对称划水方式在流体动力学上是等效且最优的，这解释了自然界中对称游泳步态的普遍性。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 高效运动对复杂生命的演化至关重要，然而选择特定游动模式（stroke）的物理原理常与生物约束条件相互交织。在黏性流体中，扇贝定理（scallop theorem）制约着运动模式的时间组织方式，但其空间结构尚缺乏类似原理，致使自然界众多生物体中普遍存在的对称步态（symmetric gaits）缺乏物理解释。本文证明，空间对称性可作为黏性流体中提升运动效率的涌现性组织原则。通过分析不受特定对称类别约束的可变形游动体，我们发现一种流体动力学对偶性：对称与反对称运动模式具有动力学等效性，能产生完全相同的运动速度与效率，且我们证明其在所有运动模式中达到最优。我们通过斯托克斯流（Stokes flow）的数值模拟验证了这一结论，证明该对称规则在三维形体结构中依然成立。研究结果表明，自然界中对称与交替步态的普遍存在不仅反映了发育约束，更体现了黏性环境中运动的物理最优性原则，从而与发育及神经约束机制形成了互补。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Efficient locomotion is important for the evolution of complex life, yet the physical principles selecting specific swimming strokes often remain entangled with biological constraints. In viscous fluids, the scallop theorem constrains the temporal organization of strokes, but no analogous principle is known for their spatial structure, leaving the prevalence of symmetric gaits across diverse organisms without a physical explanation. Here we show that spatial symmetry acts as an emergent organizing principle for efficiency in viscous fluids. By analysing deformable swimmers whose strokes are not constrained to any particular symmetry class, we identify a hydrodynamic duality: symmetric and anti-symmetric strokes are dynamically equivalent, yielding identical speeds and efficiencies, which we prove are optimal among all strokes. We validate this using numerical simulations of Stokes flow, demonstrating that these symmetry rules persist even in three-dimensional body plans. Our results suggest that the prevalence of symmetric and alternating gaits in nature reflects not merely a developmental constraint, but a physical optimality principle for locomotion in viscous environments, complementing developmental and neural constraints.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: hydrodynamics, swimming strategies, viscous fluids, symmetry, Stokes flow, locomotion efficiency, biological physics, optimality principle

---

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文提出了一种基于神经贝叶斯估计器和递归神经网络的摊销系统发育动力学推断方法，用于直接从重建的系统发育树估计流行病动态参数（如繁殖数、流行率），在模拟研究中表现出良好的预测性能，相比传统方法计算成本更低。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 系统发生动力学用于从病原体的系统发生树或基因组序列中推断流行病动态，但对于复杂模型而言，其所需的似然计算可能具有挑战性。本文提出了一种用于关键流行病学参数估计的神经贝叶斯估计器：该估计器可推断随时间变化的再生数、流行率和累计感染数。通过在树空间上进行分位数回归，神经贝叶斯估计器使我们能够直接从重建的系统发生树中估计后验中位数和可信区间。我们的方法采用递归神经网络作为树嵌入网络，并构建以时间和分位数水平为条件的预测网络来生成估计值。在模拟研究中，神经贝叶斯估计器展现出良好的预测性能，且不确定性估计较为保守。与BEAST2的固定树分析相比，在我们的测试场景中，神经贝叶斯估计器对时变再生数的估计偏差更小。在采样模型设定错误的情况下，神经贝叶斯估计器的性能（如预期般）有所下降但仍保持合理水平；通过对预训练模型进行微调，所得估计结果与从头训练的模型相当，而计算成本显著降低。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Phylodynamics is used to estimate epidemic dynamics from phylogenetic trees or genomic sequences of pathogens, but the likelihood calculations needed can be challenging for complex models. We present a neural Bayes estimator (NBE) for key epidemic quantities: the reproduction number, prevalence, and cumulative infections through time. By performing quantile regression over tree space, the NBE allows us to estimate posterior medians and credible intervals directly from a reconstructed tree. Our approach uses a recursive neural network as a tree embedding network with a prediction network conditioned on time and quantile level to generate the estimates. In simulation studies, the NBE achieves good predictive performance, with conservative uncertainty estimates. Compared with a BEAST2 fixed-tree analysis, the NBE gives less biased estimates of time-varying reproduction numbers in our test setting. Under a misspecified sampling model, the NBE performance degrades (as expected) but remains reasonable, and fine-tuning a pre-trained model yields estimates comparable to those from a model trained from scratch, at substantially lower computational cost.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: phylodynamics, neural Bayes estimator, recursive neural network, epidemic dynamics, reproduction number, phylogenetic trees, quantile regression, computational inference

---

### 232. ❌ Neural Control and Learning of Simulated Hand Movements With an EMG-Based Closed-Loop Interface

**作者**: Balint K. Hodossy, Dario Farina
**期刊/来源**: arxiv

**评分理由**: 论文研究的是基于EMG的闭环接口模拟手部运动的神经控制与学习，属于神经工程、生物信号处理和计算神经科学领域。虽然涉及AI（强化学习）和模拟，但核心内容与医学影像分析无关：未处理CT/MRI/超声等医学影像，不涉及图像分割、疾病诊断、预后预测、手术规划或多模态医学影像融合。所有关键词均聚焦医学影像分析，因此相关度均为0。

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该研究开发了一个结合肌肉骨骼模拟、强化学习和在线肌电信号合成的硅内神经力学模型，用于模拟手部运动控制，以评估神经控制器、增强训练数据集并为神经系统疾病生成合成数据。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 面对不确定性时，标准工程学方法通常是建模。将经过良好校准的模型数据与真实记录相结合，已在人工智能的诸多应用领域——从计算机视觉到自动驾驶——带来突破性进展。这类基于模型的数据增强方法如今也开始在生物信号处理中展现出有前景的结果。然而，尽管这些模拟数据是必要的，但对于虚拟神经生理学实验而言，它们尚不充分。仅生成能复现预定运动行为的神经信号，并不能捕捉在控制任务中探究神经机制所需的灵活性、变异性和因果结构。
> 
> 本研究提出了一种硅内神经力学模型，该模型结合了完全前向的肌肉骨骼模拟、强化学习以及序列化的在线肌电信号合成。该框架不仅提供同步的运动学、动力学及相应的神经活动，还明确模拟了虚拟受试者的前馈与反馈控制机制。通过这种方式，可以在模拟人类通过习得的强化学习策略响应神经接口并调整其行为时，呈现在线控制问题。例如，虚拟用户可学会对抗扰动的稳健手部运动，或实现对虚拟手势解码器的控制。我们通过在手部生物力学模型中进行手势任务的示例来阐述该方法，并为运用该技术评估神经控制器、增强训练数据集以及生成神经系统疾病的合成数据奠定了基础。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> The standard engineering approach when facing uncertainty is modelling. Mixing data from a well-calibrated model with real recordings has led to breakthroughs in many applications of AI, from computer vision to autonomous driving. This type of model-based data augmentation is now beginning to show promising results in biosignal processing as well. However, while these simulated data are necessary, they are not sufficient for virtual neurophysiological experiments. Simply generating neural signals that reproduce a predetermined motor behaviour does not capture the flexibility, variability, and causal structure required to probe neural mechanisms during control tasks.
>   In this study, we present an in silico neuromechanical model that combines a fully forward musculoskeletal simulation, reinforcement learning, and sequential, online electromyography synthesis. This framework provides not only synchronised kinematics, dynamics, and corresponding neural activity, but also explicitly models feedback and feedforward control in a virtual participant. In this way, online control problems can be represented, as the simulated human adapts its behaviour via a learned RL policy in response to a neural interface. For example, the virtual user can learn hand movements robust to perturbations or the control of a virtual gesture decoder. We illustrate the approach using a gesturing task within a biomechanical hand model, and lay the groundwork for using this technique to evaluate neural controllers, augment training datasets, and generate synthetic data for neurological conditions.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: neuromechanical model, musculoskeletal simulation, reinforcement learning, electromyography synthesis, hand movement control, neural interface, synthetic data generation, virtual neurophysiological experiments

### 233. ❌ Learning When to Look: On-Demand Keypoint-Video Fusion for Animal Behavior Analysis

**作者**: Weihan Li, Jingyang Ke, Yule Wang, Chengrui Li, Anqi Wu

**评分理由**: 论文研究动物行为分析，使用视频和关键点数据进行多模态融合，旨在提高计算效率。所有评分关键词均针对医学影像分析、临床诊断、手术规划等医疗应用，而本文研究对象是动物行为，属于神经科学/计算机视觉领域，与医疗影像完全无关。因此所有关键词相关度均为0分。

<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    本文提出LookAgain多模态框架，通过按需视觉融合解决动物行为分析中关键点方法的几何模糊性和视频方法的高计算成本问题，在保持性能的同时显著降低计算开销。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 从视频中理解动物行为对神经科学研究至关重要。现代实验室通常收集两种互补的数据流：来自姿态估计工具的骨骼关键点与原始视频记录。基于关键点的方法效率高，但存在几何模糊性、环境感知缺失以及对遮挡敏感等问题。基于视频的方法能捕捉丰富背景信息，但需要逐帧处理，对于现代实验产生的数百小时记录而言并不实用。我们提出LookAgain，这是一个通过按需视觉定位将关键点效率与视频表征能力相结合的多模态框架。在训练阶段，LookAgain利用密集视觉特征预训练运动编码器，并训练一个学习识别哪些帧需要视觉背景的门控模块。在推理阶段，该门控模块仅在关键点信号存在模糊性时激活视觉处理，同时保持与使用全部帧相当的性能。在单动物与多动物基准测试上的实验表明，LookAgain以显著降低的计算成本实现了强劲性能，使得对长时间记录进行高质量行为分析成为可能。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Understanding animal behavior from video is essential for neuroscience research. Modern laboratories typically collect two complementary data streams: skeletal keypoints from pose estimation tools and raw video recordings. Keypoint-based methods are efficient but suffer from geometric ambiguity, environmental blindness, and sensitivity to occlusions. Video-based methods capture rich context but require processing every frame, making them impractical for the hundreds of hours of recordings that modern experiments produce. We introduce LookAgain, a multimodal framework that combines the efficiency of keypoints with the representational power of video through on-demand visual grounding. During training, LookAgain uses dense visual features to pretrain a motion encoder and to train a gating module that learns which frames require visual context. During inference, this gating module activates visual processing only when keypoint signals are ambiguous, while maintaining performance comparable to using all frames. Experiments on single-animal and multi-animal benchmarks show that LookAgain achieves strong performance with significantly reduced computational cost, enabling high-quality behavior analysis on long-duration recordings.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: animal behavior analysis, multimodal fusion, keypoint-video fusion, on-demand visual grounding, computational efficiency, pose estimation, motion encoder, gating module

### 234. ❌ Minority-Triggered Reorientations Yield Macroscopic Cascades and Enhanced Responsiveness in Swarms

**作者**: Simon Syga, Chandraniva Guha Ray, Josué Manik Nava-Sedeño, Fernando Peruani, Andreas Deutsch
**期刊/来源**: arxiv

**评分理由**: 论文研究的是动物和细胞群体运动的集体行为机制（少数触发重定向规则），属于生物物理学、复杂系统和集体行为领域。论文内容完全不涉及医学图像分析、深度学习、疾病诊断、手术规划或任何医疗应用。所有关键词都与医学影像和临床决策支持相关，而该论文专注于理论生物模型和集体运动动力学，因此所有关键词相关度均为0分。

<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文研究动物和细胞群体运动中快速重定向的机制，提出了一种少数触发重定向规则，该规则能在保持群体凝聚力的同时显著增强集体响应能力，并产生重定向的级联效应。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 动物与细胞的集体运动常表现出快速重定向及无标度速度相关性。这使得信息能在群体中迅速传播，从而实现对环境变化及捕食者等威胁的充分集体响应。为解释此现象，我们提出一种简单且生物学上合理的机制：少数触发重定向规则。当局部有序性较高时，个体有时会追随一个显著偏离方向的邻居，而非跟随多数。与传统集群模型相比，该规则在宏观上显著改变了系统行为，因其能在广泛参数范围内产生重定向的重尾级联效应。我们的机制在保持凝聚力的同时显著增强了集体响应能力，因为局部方向性信号会引发放大的群体级重定向。本研究结果为理解集群过程中类临界涨落与高响应性提供了一条简约且具生物学可解释的路径。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Collective motion in animals and cells often exhibits rapid reorientations and scale-free velocity correlations. This allows information to spread rapidly through the group, allowing an adequate collective response to environmental changes and threats such as predators. To explain this phenomenon, we introduce a simple, biologically plausible mechanism: a minority-triggered reorientation rule. When local order is high, agents sometimes follow a strongly deviating neighbor instead of the majority. This rule qualitatively changes the macroscopic system behavior compared to traditional flocking models, as it generates heavy-tailed cascades of reorientations over broad parameter ranges. Our mechanism preserves cohesion while markedly enhancing collective responsiveness because localized directional cues elicit amplified group-level reorientation. Our results provide a parsimonious, biologically interpretable route to critical-like fluctuations and high responsiveness during flocking.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: collective motion, minority-triggered reorientation, flocking models, scale-free correlations, collective responsiveness, cascades, biological systems, agent-based modeling

### 235. ❌ Exploring Strategies for Personalized Radiation Therapy Part IV: An Interaction-Picture Approach to Quantifying the Abscopal Effect

**作者**: Hao Peng, Laurentiu Pop, Kai Jiang, Faya Zhang, Debabrata Saha, Raquibul Hannan, Robert Timmerman
**期刊/来源**: arxiv
**发布日期**: 2026-03-07
**arXiv链接**: [http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08751v1](http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08751v1)

**评分**: 0.0 / 29.0 ❌

<details>
<summary>评分详情</summary>

| 关键词 | 权重 | 相关度 | 得分 |
|------|------|------|------|
| medical image analysis | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| medical image segmentation | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| deep learning medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| AI for diagnosis | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| prognosis prediction | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| surgical planning | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| multimodal medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| foundation models medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文研究个性化放射治疗中的远隔效应量化方法，使用量子力学中的相互作用图像变换来分离肿瘤生长与辐射/免疫扰动。研究内容聚焦于放射治疗机制、数学模型和免疫反应，完全不涉及医学影像分析、分割、深度学习、AI诊断、预后预测、手术规划、多模态影像或基础模型等关键词。所有关键词与论文主题无直接关联。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该研究提出了一种基于量子力学相互作用图像变换的数学模型，用于量化个性化超分割立体定向自适应放疗中的远隔效应，并在两种临床前双侧肿瘤模型中验证了该方法能捕捉个体水平的肿瘤间相互作用动态。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 我们在个性化超分割立体定向自适应放射治疗（Personalized Ultra-Fractionated Stereotactic Adaptive Radiotherapy，简称PULSAR）的背景下，重新审视了具有争议性的“远隔效应”。与传统每日分割放疗相比，PULSAR允许更长的分次间隔时间，这可能增强全身性免疫激活，并提高远隔效应发生的可能性。为了量化治疗诱导的效应，我们引入了一种借鉴自量子力学的相互作用绘景变换方法，该方法将肿瘤的内在生长与放疗及免疫介导的扰动分离开来。在这项初步研究中，我们将此方法应用于两种临床前双侧肿瘤模型（4T1和MC38）。我们的模型提供了一种在个体层面量化原发肿瘤与继发肿瘤之间相互作用强度的测量方法，能够捕捉随时间变化的动态过程，而非仅仅依赖队列平均值。这种方法将远隔效应定义为一个连续的、随机的现象，而非二元反应。该框架具有灵活性，适用于未来研究，特别是在PULSAR联合放疗与免疫治疗中，可用于比较不同放疗剂量和分割方案，并可纳入免疫检查点抑制剂（Immune Checkpoint Inhibitors, ICIs）以进一步增强全身性抗肿瘤免疫。该框架还有助于我们进行跨研究的远隔效应比较，并标准化远隔效应强度的报告方式，而不仅仅是简单的统计学显著性。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> We revisit the controversial "abscopal" effect in the context of Personalized Ultra-Fractionated Stereotactic Adaptive Radiotherapy (PULSAR). By allowing long interval between fractions, PULSAR may enhance systemic immune activation and increase the likelihood of abscopal responses compared with conventional daily fractionation. To quantify treatment-induced effects, we introduce an interaction-picture transformation adapted from quantum mechanics, which separates intrinsic tumor growth from radiation and immune-mediated perturbations. In this preliminary study, we tested this method to two preclinical bilateral tumor models (4T1 and MC38). Our model provides a quantitative measure of the interaction strength between primary and secondary tumors at the individual level, capturing dynamics over time rather than relying solely on cohort averages. This approach frames the abscopal effect as a continuous, stochastic phenomenon rather than a binary response. The framework is flexible for future studies, particularly in concurrent radiation and immunotherapy with PULSAR, where different radiation doses and fractionation schedules can be compared, and immune checkpoint inhibitors (ICIs) can be incorporated to further enhance systemic anti-tumor immunity. The framework can also help us make cross-study comparison of abscopal effects and standardizes the reporting of abscopal magnitude beyond simple statistical significance.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: abscopal effect, personalized radiation therapy, PULSAR, interaction-picture transformation, tumor growth modeling, immune activation, quantitative measurement, preclinical tumor models

---

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 肥胖并非骤然发生，而是长期逐渐形成的。这种渐进过程常使人们难以在脂肪过度积累前早期识别生理变化。一种普遍观点认为，只需"少吃多动"即可实现减重。尽管减少热量摄入与增加体力活动是体重管理的基本原则，这种观点过度简化了一个复杂且具有适应性的生物系统。代谢率、激素调节、行为因素及代偿性生理反应均影响着机体对体重变化的抵抗机制。在减重过程中，代谢率下降与能量利用效率提升使得维持热量赤字日益困难。反之，在过度摄食期间，随着体重上升，静息代谢率、食物热效应和非运动活动产热均会增强，从而部分抵消热量盈余并减缓体重增长。然而，这些代偿反应具有不对称性——相较于过度摄食，机体对营养不足的适应机制更强且更持久。这种不对称性有助于解释为何体重增长常呈渐进趋势，以及为何持续减重在生物学层面面临挑战。本研究采用动力系统理论中的λ-ω模型（lambda-omega model）来描述代谢系统对生活方式扰动的调控响应。我们引入时变参数，使调节系数能够在持续的环境与生理压力下逐步演变。通过允许λ(t)和ω(t)随时间变化，该模型能够捕捉代谢设定点的渐进性偏移及底层动力学图景的形变。此框架可用于探索代谢状态间的转换，以及影响体重增减轨迹的长期适应机制。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Obesity does not emerge abruptly; rather, it develops gradually over extended periods. The gradual progression often prevents early recognition of physiological changes until excess adiposity is established. A common belief is that weight reduction can be achieved simply by "eating less and moving more". Although reductions in caloric intake and increases in physical activity are fundamental principles of weight management, this perspective oversimplifies a complex and adaptive biological system. Metabolic rate, hormonal regulation, behavioral factors, and compensatory physiological responses all influence the body's resistance to changes in weight. During weight loss, reduced metabolic rate and increased efficiency make maintaining a caloric deficit increasingly difficult. Conversely, during periods of overfeeding, resting metabolic rate, the thermic effect of food, and non-exercise activity thermogenesis increase with rising body weight, partially offsetting the caloric surplus and slowing weight gain. However, these compensatory responses are asymmetrical, with stronger and more persistent adaptations to underfeeding than to overfeeding. This asymmetry helps explain why weight gain often occurs gradually and why sustained weight loss is biologically challenging. In this work, we employ a lambda-omega model from dynamical systems theory to describe metabolic regulation in response to lifestyle perturbations. We introduce time-varying parameters that allow the regulatory coefficients to evolve gradually under sustained environmental and physiological stressors. By allowing lambda(t) and omega(t) to vary over time, the model captures progressive shifts in the metabolic set-point and deformation of the underlying dynamical landscape. This framework enables exploration of transitions between metabolic states and long-term adaptations that shape trajectories of weight gain and loss.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: obesity, metabolic regulation, dynamical systems, lambda-omega model, weight loss, physiological compensation, time-varying parameters, metabolic state transitions

---

### 237. ❌ A recipe for scalable attention-based MLIPs: unlocking long-range accuracy with all-to-all node attention

**作者**: Eric Qu, Brandon M. Wood, Aditi S. Krishnapriyan, Zachary W. Ulissi
**期刊/来源**: arxiv
**发布日期**: 2026-03-06
**arXiv链接**: [http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06567v1](http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06567v1)

**评分**: 0.0 / 29.0 ❌

**评分理由**: 该论文研究的是机器学习原子间势能（MLIPs）模型，专注于分子系统、材料和催化剂的物理模拟，通过注意力机制解决长程相互作用问题。论文内容完全属于计算化学、分子模拟和材料科学领域，与医学图像分析、临床决策支持、疾病诊断、手术规划等医疗AI主题没有任何关联。所有关键词均与论文研究内容无关。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文提出了一种基于注意力机制的可扩展机器学习原子间势能模型AllScAIP，通过全节点注意力组件解决了长程相互作用问题，在分子系统上实现了最先进的能量/力预测精度，并支持稳定的长时间尺度分子动力学模拟。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 机器学习原子间势（MLIPs）发展迅速，许多顶尖模型依赖于基于物理的强归纳偏置。然而，当模型扩展到生物分子和电解质等更大体系时，它们难以准确捕捉长程（LR）相互作用，导致当前方法依赖于显式的基于物理的项或组件。在本工作中，我们提出了AllScAIP，一个简洁、基于注意力机制且能量守恒的MLIP模型，其训练规模可扩展至O(1亿)个样本。它通过一种数据驱动的全节点注意力组件来解决长程挑战。广泛的消融实验表明，在低数据/小模型条件下，归纳偏置能提高样本效率。但随着数据和模型规模的扩大，这些优势会减弱甚至逆转，而全节点注意力对于捕捉长程相互作用仍然至关重要。我们的模型在分子体系上实现了最先进的能量/力预测精度，并在多项基于物理的评估（OMol25）中表现出色，同时在材料（OMat24）和催化剂（OC20）体系上也具有竞争力。此外，它支持稳定、长时标的分子动力学（MD）模拟，能准确复现实验观测值，包括密度和汽化热的预测。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Machine-learning interatomic potentials (MLIPs) have advanced rapidly, with many top models relying on strong physics-based inductive biases. However, as models scale to larger systems like biomolecules and electrolytes, they struggle to accurately capture long-range (LR) interactions, leading current approaches to rely on explicit physics-based terms or components. In this work, we propose AllScAIP, a straightforward, attention-based, and energy-conserving MLIP model that scales to O(100 million) training samples. It addresses the long-range challenge using an all-to-all node attention component that is data-driven. Extensive ablations reveal that in low-data/small-model regimes, inductive biases improve sample efficiency. However, as data and model size scale, these benefits diminish or even reverse, while all-to-all attention remains critical for capturing LR interactions. Our model achieves state-of-the-art energy/force accuracy on molecular systems, as well as a number of physics-based evaluations (OMol25), while being competitive on materials (OMat24) and catalysts (OC20). Furthermore, it enables stable, long-timescale MD simulations that accurately recover experimental observables, including density and heat of vaporization predictions.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: machine-learning interatomic potentials, attention-based model, long-range interactions, all-to-all node attention, molecular dynamics simulations, energy/force accuracy, scalable MLIPs, materials and catalysts

### 238. ❌ GWAS Summary Statistic Tool: A Meta-Analysis and Parsing Tool for Polygenic Risk Score Calculation

**作者**: Muhammad Muneeb, David B. Ascher
**期刊/来源**: arxiv
**发布日期**: 2026-03-06
**arXiv链接**: [http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06756v1](http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06756v1)

**评分**: 0.0 / 29.0 ❌

| prognosis prediction | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文主题是基因组学工具开发，专注于GWAS摘要统计文件的元分析和解析，用于多基因风险评分计算。所有评分关键词均涉及医学影像分析、深度学习、AI诊断、预后预测、手术规划等医学影像领域，而论文完全不涉及任何医学影像内容，因此所有关键词相关度均为0分。

<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文开发了GWASPoker工具，通过部分下载和头部检测自动筛选GWAS摘要统计文件，解决了手动处理文件耗时耗存储的问题，成功处理了GWAS Catalog中绝大多数记录。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 研究动机：全基因组关联研究（GWAS）摘要统计量文件是多基因风险评分（PRS）计算的关键输入数据。然而，从数千条目录条目中识别合适的文件通常需要下载大型数据集并人工检查其列结构，这一过程既耗时又占用大量存储空间。
> 
> 研究结果：我们开发了GWASPoker，这是一个表型驱动的、专门针对GWAS目录的预下载筛选工具。它通过部分下载和表头检测来扫描候选GWAS文件，以判断其是否包含PRS计算所需的列，而无需完整传输文件。通过对GWAS目录中60,499条记录的分析，其中60,281条（99.6%）包含可访问的下载链接；在这之中，54,026条（89.6%）记录的文件成功实现了部分下载和解析，涵盖了20种文件格式，并产生了724种独特的表头特征。在13种表型类别中，85个经人工整理的GWAS文件中有84个（98.8%）被自动检索并处理。与完整下载文件进行的表头验证显示，28个案例中有23个（82.1%）完全一致。
> 
> 可用性与实现：GWASPoker采用Python 3编写，在MIT许可下可于https://github.com/MuhammadMuneeb007/GWASPokerforPRS 免费获取。代码库中提供了示例输出和文档。该工具在Linux（高性能计算集群）环境下使用Python 3.8或更高版本进行了测试。其中基于大语言模型（LLM）的代码生成步骤完全可选；工具同时提供了一个基于规则的列映射模板，支持完全离线使用。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Motivation: GWAS (genome-wide association study) summary statistic files are essential inputs for polygenic risk score (PRS) calculation. However, identifying suitable files across thousands of catalog entries typically requires downloading large datasets and manually inspecting their column structures, a process that is both time-consuming and storage-intensive.
>   Results: We present GWASPoker, a phenotype-driven, GWAS-Catalog-specific pre-download triage tool that scans candidate GWAS files for PRS column availability through partial downloads and header detection, without requiring full-file transfer. Analysing 60,499 records from the GWAS Catalog, 60,281 (99.6%) contained accessible download links, of which 54,026 (89.6%) were successfully partially downloaded and parsed across 20 file formats, yielding 724 unique header signatures. Across 13 phenotypes, 84 of 85 manually curated GWAS files (98.8%) were automatically retrieved and processed. Header validation against fully downloaded files showed exact agreement in 23 of 28 cases (82.1%).
>   Availability and implementation: GWASPoker is implemented in Python 3 and is freely available at https://github.com/MuhammadMuneeb007/GWASPokerforPRS  under the MIT licence. Example outputs and documentation are provided in the repository. The tool was tested on Linux (HPC cluster) with Python 3.8 or later. The LLM-based code-generation step is entirely optional; a rules-based column-mapping template is provided for fully offline use.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: GWAS, polygenic risk score, summary statistics, meta-analysis, GWAS Catalog, header detection, Python tool, PRS calculation

### 239. ❌ Multicellular Tumour Spheroids Exposure to Pulsed Electric Field: A Combined Experimental and Mathematical Modelling Study Highlighting Temporal Dynamics of DAMP Release and Accelerated Regrowth at Intermediate Field Intensities

**作者**: Emma Leschiera, Nicolas Mattei, Marie-Pierre Rols, Muriel Golzio, Jelena Kolosnjaj-Tabi, Clair Poignard
**期刊/来源**: arxiv

**评分理由**: 论文研究电穿孔技术对肿瘤球体的影响，结合实验和数学模型分析细胞死亡、DAMP释放和肿瘤再生长的动态过程。所有评分关键词均涉及医学影像分析、深度学习、AI诊断、预后预测、手术规划、多模态影像或基础模型，而本文完全不涉及医学影像处理、AI算法开发或临床决策支持系统，属于肿瘤生物物理学和计算生物学领域，与所有关键词完全无关。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    本研究通过实验和数学模型探究电穿孔强度对肿瘤球体再生、细胞死亡和免疫原性细胞死亡相关分子释放的动态影响，发现中等强度脉冲会导致加速再生并强调静止细胞的双重作用。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 电穿孔技术作为一种经皮消融手段，正日益广泛地应用于邻近重要结构的肿瘤治疗。尽管该技术有效，但肿瘤再生仍可能发生。同时，针对单层细胞培养的体外研究表明，电穿孔可通过释放损伤相关分子模式（Damage-Associated Molecular Patterns, DAMPs）引发免疫原性细胞死亡（Immunogenic Cell Death, ICD）。这些分子能够激活免疫系统，从而可能抑制肿瘤再生。为充分发挥电穿孔的潜力，必须解决两个关键问题：（1）肿瘤再生的动态驱动机制是什么；（2）ICD在三维细胞结构（其比二维培养更能模拟体内环境）中如何随空间和时间展开。本研究结合体外实验与基于个体/连续的混合计算模型，以探究不同脉冲强度下肿瘤球体的再生能力及ICD潜力。实验量化了球体活力、生长速率以及ATP和HMGB1的释放情况。与此同时，混合模型预测了增殖细胞、静息细胞和坏死细胞的动态变化。两种方法均表明，细胞死亡与DAMP释放程度随脉冲强度增加而增强。经实验数据验证的模型进一步揭示了静息细胞的双重作用：部分细胞死亡并释放空间与资源，而其他细胞则存活并恢复增殖。这些发现共同阐明了球体命运如何取决于脉冲强度，并强调了在设计基于电穿孔的治疗方案时考虑静息细胞的重要性。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Electroporation is increasingly used as a percutaneous ablation technique for tumours located near vital structures. Although effective, tumour regrowth may still occur. At the same time, in vitro studies on cell monolayers have shown that electroporation can trigger immunogenic cell death (ICD) through the release of damage-associated molecular patterns (DAMPs). These molecules can stimulate the immune system and could counteract tumour regrowth. To fully exploit electroporation, two key questions must be addressed: (1) what dynamics drive tumour regrowth, and (2) how ICD unfolds in space and time within three-dimensional cellular structures, which better mimic in vivo conditions than 2D cultures. Here, we combine in vitro experiments with a hybrid individual-based/continuous computational model to explore tumour spheroid regrowth and ICD potential under different pulse intensities. Experiments quantify spheroid viability, growth rate, and the release of ATP and HMGB1. In parallel, the hybrid model predicts the dynamics of proliferative, quiescent, and necrotic cells. Both approaches show that cell death and DAMP release scale with pulse intensity. The model, validated against experimental data, further highlights the dual role of quiescent cells: some die and free space and resources, while others survive and resume proliferation. Together, these findings demonstrate how spheroid fate depends on pulse strength and emphasize the importance of accounting for quiescent cells when designing electroporation-based therapies.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: electroporation, tumor spheroids, immunogenic cell death, DAMP release, computational modeling, pulse intensity, quiescent cells, tumor regrowth
