!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文提出了ViroGym基准，用于评估病毒蛋白质的变体效应预测，并利用蛋白质语言模型和实验数据指导抗原选择，以改进疫苗开发。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 蛋白质语言模型（pLMs）在零样本设置下已展现出预测错义变异功能效应的强大潜力。尽管取得这一进展，针对病毒蛋白质的pLMs基准测试仍然有限，且将计算指标与体外验证相结合以指导抗原和靶点选择的系统性策略尚不完善。本文提出ViroGym——一个旨在评估病毒蛋白质变异效应预测并促进合理抗原候选物筛选的综合基准平台。我们整合了79项涵盖真核病毒深度突变扫描（DMS）实验数据，共包含7种不同表型读数下的552,937个突变氨基酸序列，以及21项流感病毒中和任务和一项针对SARS-CoV-2的现实世界预测任务。通过在适应度景观、抗原多样性和大流行预测方面对成熟pLMs进行基准测试，我们构建了一个疫苗筛选框架，并证明利用体外实验数据筛选的pLMs能出色预测现实世界中流行的主要突变。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Protein language models (pLMs) have shown strong potential in prediction of the functional effects of missense variants in zero-shot settings. Despite this progress, benchmarking pLMs for viral proteins remains limited and systematic strategies for integrating in silico metrics with in vitro validation to guide antigen and target selection are underdeveloped. Here, we introduce ViroGym, a comprehensive benchmark designed to evaluate variant effect prediction in viral proteins and to facilitate selecting rational antigen candidates. We curated 79 deep mutational scanning (DMS) assays encompassing eukaryotic viruses, collectively comprising 552,937 mutated amino acid sequences across 7 distinct phenotypic readouts, and 21 influenza virus neutralisation tasks and a real-world predictive task for SARS-CoV-2. We benchmark well-established pLMs on fitness landscapes, antigenic diversity, and pandemic forecasting to provide a framework for vaccine selection, and show that pLMs selected using in vitro experimental data excel at predicting dominant circulating mutations in real world.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: ViroGym, viral proteins, protein language models, variant effect prediction, deep mutational scanning, antigen selection, vaccine development, benchmark evaluation

**评分理由**: 论文研究的是神经科学领域的钙成像数据分析方法（INTENSE框架），用于检测和解析神经元对行为变量的选择性。所有评分关键词均针对医学影像分析、疾病诊断、手术规划等临床应用，而本文专注于基础神经科学研究，使用钙成像技术分析小鼠神经元活动与行为的关系，不涉及任何医学影像（如CT、MRI、超声）、疾病诊断、预后预测或临床决策支持。因此，所有关键词与论文内容完全无关，得分为0。

<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    本文提出了INTENSE框架，利用互信息从钙成像数据中检测和解析神经元对行为变量的选择性，解决了钙动力学和时间自相关带来的分析挑战，并在小鼠实验中验证了其有效性。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 神经元通过其活动编码环境信息。当动物探索环境时，神经元会迅速对外部世界的不同特征产生选择性；刻画这些选择性模式如何出现、重组和重叠，是将神经活动与行为及认知联系起来的关键。在自由行为动物中进行钙成像可以记录大规模神经元群体，但由于信号均存在时间自相关性且钙动力学会引入时间延迟，直接从连续荧光信号中量化神经元-行为选择性具有挑战性。
> 
> 本文提出INTENSE（神经元选择性的信息论评估框架），这是一个基于互信息从原始钙荧光数据中检测神经元-行为关联的开源框架。INTENSE通过保留时间结构的循环移位置换检验来控制错误发现，并优化时间延迟以考虑指示剂动力学及前瞻性/回顾性编码。为区分真实的混合选择性与由行为协方差驱动的关联，INTENSE采用基于条件互信息的解耦方法。
> 
> 我们在合成数据集上验证了INTENSE，证明其能在不同信噪比和可靠性条件下实现稳健检测，而缺乏时间控制的方法则表现不佳。将INTENSE应用于小鼠自由探索开放场时的CA1区微型显微镜记录，该框架揭示了对多个变量（位置、头部方向、物体交互、运动状态）的稳健选择性，并通过区分冗余编码与真正的多变量编码，优化了混合选择性的估计。综上，INTENSE实现了高通量、信息论驱动的选择性映射，其具备对时间结构和行为协方差的原理性控制，为从大规模记录到环路水平假说的构建搭建了桥梁。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Neurons encode information about the environment through their activity. As animals explore the environment, neurons rapidly acquire selectivity for distinct features of the external world; characterizing how these selectivity patterns emerge, reorganize, and overlap is key to linking neural activity to behavior and cognition. Calcium imaging in freely behaving animals can record large neuronal populations, but quantifying neuron-behavior selectivity directly from continuous fluorescence is challenging because both signals are temporally autocorrelated and calcium kinetics introduce time lags.
>   Here we present INTENSE (INformation-Theoretic Evaluation of Neuronal SElectivity), an open-source framework that uses mutual information to detect neuron-behavior associations from raw calcium fluorescence data. INTENSE controls false discoveries using circular-shift permutation testing that preserves temporal structure and optimizes temporal delays to account for indicator kinetics and prospective/retrospective encoding. To separate genuine mixed selectivity from associations driven by behavioral covariance, INTENSE applies conditional mutual information-based disentanglement.
>   We validated INTENSE on synthetic datasets, demonstrating robust detection across diverse signal-to-noise ratios and reliability conditions, whereas methods lacking temporal controls show poor performance. Applied to CA1 miniscope recordings in mice freely exploring an open field, INTENSE reveals robust selectivity to multiple variables (place, head direction, object interaction, locomotion) and refines mixed-selectivity estimates by distinguishing redundant from genuinely multi-variable encoding. Together, INTENSE enables high-throughput, information-theoretic selectivity mapping with principled control of temporal structure and behavioral covariance, bridging large-scale recordings to circuit-level hypotheses.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: calcium imaging, neuronal selectivity, mutual information, behavior analysis, neural encoding, information theory, temporal autocorrelation, mixed selectivity

### 242. ❌ A Modelling Assessment of the Impact of Control Measures on Simulated Foot-and-Mouth Disease Spread in Mato Grosso do Sul, Brazil

**作者**: Nicolas C. Cardenas, Jacqueline Marques de Oliveira, Andre de Medeiros C. Lins, Fernando Endrigo Ramos Garcia, Marcus Vinicius Angelo, Robson Campos dos Anjos, Fabricio de Lima Weber, Frederico Bittencourt Fernandes Maia, Vanessa Felipe de Souza, Gustavo Machado

**评分理由**: 论文研究的是口蹄疫（FMD）在巴西马托格罗索州的传播模拟与控制策略评估，属于兽医流行病学领域，使用基于易感-暴露-感染-恢复（SEIR）的数学模型。所有评分关键词均聚焦于医学影像分析、深度学习、AI诊断、手术规划等医学影像与人工智能临床决策支持领域，而本文完全不涉及医学影像、图像处理、深度学习或任何形式的影像数据，因此所有关键词相关度均为0分。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该研究通过模拟口蹄疫在巴西马托格罗索州的传播，评估了不同控制策略（如疫苗接种和扑杀）的效果，发现单独高疫苗接种效果最差，而高扑杀能力结合有限疫苗接种能100%控制疫情且用时最短。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 本研究模拟了口蹄疫（Foot-and-mouth disease, FMD）传入巴西马托格罗索州的情景，以评估疫情控制策略的有效性。我们利用易感-潜伏-感染-恢复模型，模拟出该州范围内不同规模的疫情暴发情况。基于这些模拟疫情，我们评估了六种防控情景的效果：高密度疫苗接种、两种中等规模扑杀结合疫苗接种的变体方案、有限疫苗接种配合高强度扑杀，以及单独实施中等强度和高强度扑杀。结果显示，仅依靠高密度疫苗接种是效果最差的策略，仅能控制2.22%的疫情暴发，且导致感染农场数量最多、控制持续时间最长。采用中等规模扑杀结合疫苗接种的混合策略可控制约91%的疫情。单独实施中等规模扑杀可控制96.60%的疫情，且比混合策略快14-15天完成控制。最有效的策略是将最高强度扑杀能力与有限疫苗接种相结合，可控制100%的疫情，且控制周期最短。不同策略下的疫苗接种动物数量差异显著：最优策略需接种211,002头，而仅采用疫苗接种策略时需接种596,530头。本研究证明，仅靠疫苗接种不足以消除疫情，未来在马托格罗索州防控口蹄疫传入需结合扑杀与疫苗接种策略。此类成功策略可在10至15天内消除90%至100%的疫情，并将感染农场数量减少10至13个。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> This study simulated the introduction of Foot-and-mouth disease (FMD) into Mato Grosso do Sul, Brazil, to evaluate the effectiveness of outbreak control strategies. Our susceptible-exposed-infected-recovered model generated a range of outbreak sizes across the state. These outbreaks were used to model control actions across six scenarios: high vaccination, two variations of moderate depopulation combined with vaccination, high depopulation with limited vaccination, and moderate and high depopulation alone. Our results showed that relying solely on high vaccination was the least effective approach; it controlled only 2.22 % of outbreaks and resulted in the highest number of infected farms and the longest control duration. Mixed strategies, busing, moderate depopulation, and vaccination controlled approximately 91 % of outbreaks. The use of moderate depopulation alone controlled 96.60 % of outbreaks, and it was 14-15 days faster than the mixed approaches. The most effective strategy combined the highest depopulation capacity with limited vaccination, controlling 100 % of outbreaks and producing the shortest control duration. The number of vaccinated animals ranged from 211,002 under the optimal strategy to 596,530 when the control strategy included only vaccination. We demonstrated that vaccination alone was insufficient to eliminate outbreaks, and that depopulation and vaccination strategies would be required to stamp out future FMD introduction in Mato Grosso do Sul (MS). The success of such a strategy would eliminate between 90 % to 100 % of outbreaks in 10 to 15 days and reduce the number of infected farms by 10 to 13.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: Foot-and-mouth disease, outbreak simulation, control strategies, vaccination, depopulation, SEIR model, Mato Grosso do Sul, epidemiological modeling
